                   President of the World Peace Unification Family, Hwang Seon-jo

1)
Complete Restoration
<Prayer> Beloved Father, today is May 21, 1972, and it is the third Sabbath of this month. May Your glory be upon the children gathered here this morning. May You fulfill the new hope, new peace, and new world of unity as You desire.
The children gathered here have sworn to be completely offered as a new offering before Your will, dedicating their bodies and minds, so please accept them according to Your joyful will. Allow us to become a people and children that cannot be absent from the kingdom of glory.
Father, please bless the countless children who bow their heads in reverence to You. Not only the children scattered across the Korean Peninsula but also the many young children abroad long for this place as their spiritual homeland, so I earnestly hope and wish that Your infinite mercy and victory may be with them wherever they are, filled with tears as they yearn for You and Your victorious nation.
Father, please give us new commandments this morning. May this Sabbath, which we celebrate for the second time upon returning to our homeland, be a joy before You.
We understand that it is our mission to present a new movement under the historical plan, so Father, we hope that everything will begin with Your will and culminate within Your providence.
We know that humanity cannot achieve great purposes on its own. Through history, through the ages, and into the future, this is the principle; without Your involvement, there would be no victorious past, present, or future.
We hope that there will be many holy groups on this earth who focus on heaven, look to Your will, practice everything in accordance with Your will, and live lives that culminate all hopes in Your will. We recognize that fallen humanity is a pitiful group that must walk the sorrowful path of restoration and indemnity to be embraced once again in Your bosom.
Father, we know that only Your infinite power, mercy, and love can save our lives. Father, do not leave the pitiful ones as they are, but come to awaken our hearts, and awaken our original nature so that we may learn to yearn for You. Allow us to praise Your holiness, and awaken our hearts to admire and desire Your glorious form.
In front of Your beloved self, as those called to serve You, may we gather this morning with the heart to become a complete offering of victory before Your will, dedicating our lives and everything.
Always lacking, always insufficient, and always incomplete, may You whip us to guide us to the standard of victory. If we remain in a state of inadequacy, I earnestly hope and wish that You will lead us to overcome that hurdle, even if it means striking us with a whip.
Father, through this world tour, You have scattered the young children everywhere and allowed them to fight for new hopes and a new nation, so please be with them personally. In the places where they look forward to meeting and parting, may their longing connect with You, and may the groups that yearn for You, follow Your will or words, and praise You with songs be blessed with Your infinite mercy and victory, Father, I earnestly hope and wish.
We are not born for anyone else. We are not called for anyone else. We are solely called for You and for Your nation. We were born to be able to affirm the joyful day of victory before Your will, to become heavenly heroes that You can be proud of and that will remain in the historical journey. Therefore, we have walked the path of struggle on the road of goodness until now. In the future, we wish to run this path again, so even if we encounter loneliness or sorrow, may You be our center, our standard, and the beacon of light in the world of darkness, always shining and guiding us.
Father, please look upon our inadequate selves, remove the roots of sin that do not align with good hearts, and with Your fiery power, penetrate our hearts, and allow us to recreate the final victory. I earnestly hope and wish that You will manifest and observe us.
Father, I earnestly hope and wish that You will be with the 22 of Your children who are here representing the children scattered across Europe, protecting and blessing them. I earnestly ask and wish that all the movements they have initiated while touring the nation may be gathered before You and contribute to the foundation of Your victory.
Please allow this day to be holy. I pray all these words in the name of True Parents. Amen.
10   Complete Restoration
<Words> We know that countless people living on this earth are living in a sinful world. No matter how good a life someone may have lived, when reflecting on their life at the end, that person will inevitably discover that they have not lived as well as they could have.
Humans at the Crossroads of Good and Evil
If we were to extract the good and evil deeds from our lives one by one, we would hope that what remains in the end is good, but we come to realize that it is easier for evil to remain than good in the course of our lives.
When we consider the countless people of an era, if we remove the good and evil of each individual, and if evil remains more than good, then the people living on this earth are not good people but evil people, and this society is not a good society but an evil society.
Even when we observe the long history of humanity, which is formed by individuals connecting together, we must inherit the truth and become a history of truth, but we conclude that instead of truth, evil remains, leading to a history of evil. Therefore, we cannot help but think that this world is not a good world but an evil world.
So why has the world become so evil? If good had started first and planted the seeds of goodness, then the harvest would have been good according to what was sown. However, it is not good that has been sown, but evil has been planted first. Evil has been sown on a foundation of goodness. This is the problem. If evil had been sown on an evil foundation, it could only continue as evil, but because evil has been sown on a good foundation, the good and evil aspects are intertwined as they descend. Because evil has been sown on a good foundation, what ultimately remains is not good but evil, which we can conclude by looking at the whole. Therefore, we can understand that the world we live in today is under the dominion of evil. In other words, it is not good that governs the whole, but evil that governs it.
Humans must be evil because they started from evil, but if there is a good absolute being, what would that absolute being be like? Or if there is an absolute being, there must also be an opposing evil Satan; what kind of being is that Satan? When we think about these issues, God must be absolutely good. He must be good from the beginning, good in the process, and good at the end. This is an undeniable fact. The past He has walked, the present in which He promotes providence, and the future are not a combination of good and evil for Him, nor can good and evil appear. For Him, only good remains, and evil cannot exist. We cannot see it any other way.
What kind of being is that opposing Satan? For him, there can be no good. He is evil from the start, evil in the process, and evil in the result. If Satan could take a good position before God, wouldn't it create confusion for us humans as we seek the path of goodness? Therefore, evil must always remain in an evil position. From beginning to end, Satan must be evil. We cannot help but reach this conclusion.
We humans are caught between the good God and the opposing evil Satan. Therefore, when I pursue goodness throughout my life, the good God is with me, and when I stand in opposition, the evil Satan is with me. This is the fate of humanity today.
In the course of life, how to establish the path that can leave only goodness while yearning for the good God is what humanity hopes for above all else. Thus, we can stand on the side of the good God. If not, we will end up on the side of evil. By centering on the absolute good, we humans can only find the way to believe in God absolutely and become one with Him, so that our life journey can begin with good, go through the process of good, and bear the fruit of good. When we have lived our entire lives and remove good and evil one by one, if evil is greater than good, we will end up under the dominion of evil, and if good remains even one more than evil, we will end up under the dominion of good. This is how we see it.
Faith life is what? It is to prevent evil and leave the good in our life journey, and we must understand that this is the faith life that we humans believe in. Then what is the highest hope that we humans desire? It is to hope for complete goodness.
In Matthew 5:48, it says, "Be perfect, therefore, as your heavenly Father is perfect." If the absolute and good subject, God, truly wishes to love humanity, and if humanity can stand in the position of the object of that love, then humanity must hope to stand as a good being in relation to the absolute God. Wouldn't the relative being not want to be in a position of groaning and being accused before Satan? This is beyond question. Therefore, the God who is the subject of complete goodness wishes to be the complete objective reality of goodness for humanity.
Does He wish for this from the moment of birth? Of course, He would. Would He wish for humanity to live that way throughout their lives? Of course, He would. He has wished for this until now, and He must wish for humanity to be good in the future as well. Is it not true that God wishes for humanity to be good from the moment of birth throughout their lives? If this is true for the present and the future, then it must also be true for the past. God must have hoped for this in the past as well. Therefore, there must be efforts made by God to leave a foundation of goodness in the past. That is necessary.
What happened after Adam and Eve fell? They were supposed to remove evil themselves and determine to move to a good position, standing between God and Satan. However, because Adam and Eve themselves could not do it, the subject of goodness, God, had to intervene and establish a standard of goodness that could connect God and Adam and Eve.
What kind of place is that standard determined? It must be determined based on the highest hope that humanity desires. It is human nature to wish for happiness from the moment of birth and to wish for happiness as they grow. What is the center of that highest hope for happiness? If Adam and Eve were created in the position of children who could serve God as their parent, then the place where they could receive the greatest love as children before their parents would be the highest hope of Adam and Eve.
The issue is love. If God loves Adam and Eve, what kind of position would Adam and Eve want to be in to receive that love? Or what would be the position they hope for the most? It would be the position where they can be loved as the sons and daughters of God. What kind of love is that? It is complete love. They must receive complete love as sons and daughters.
The fact that they fell means that they did not complete the position where they could receive God's complete love throughout their lives as His children. If they had not fallen, Adam and Eve would have had the absolute God as their parent and would have received God's abundant love as children throughout their lives. If they had received complete love, they would have seen a perfect start in the history of love centered on God. Our human ancestors, who were supposed to make such a historical start, failed to do so and did not reach that point. This is the fall.
The God who is the subject of complete love created humanity to give complete love, yet that love could not be given. Therefore, it is undeniable that God must stand in a position of regret or sorrow because of fallen humanity.
We are saying that God is an absolute being, and therefore, the absolute results planned by the absolute God should also be absolute. However, due to the fall of humanity, such results could not be achieved, and although it should have started centered on absolute love, because fallen humanity could not see that beginning, it is impossible to maintain God's authority and position as the absolute God unless this is inevitably realized.

For this reason, we can conclude that God cannot help but overcome difficulties to find such standards again. The failure to see a perfect beginning centered on God's love as a son is the fall.

Then, what happens after receiving perfect love as a son? One must receive love as a perfect couple. Adam was born as a man, and Eve was born as a woman. Since they fell, if they had matured in a position of receiving perfect love without falling, that is, if they had been born and grown in the embrace of God's love and matured within God's complete love realm, they would have seen a perfect beginning as a couple that God delights in. This is beyond question.

If that had happened, would that couple have been unhappy? No. That couple would have stood in a position that the absolute God delights in, and because they became one with God's love, Adam and Eve, in a relative position centered on absolute love, could not have been anything but happy.

What God possesses can be their possessions in a relative position, and the joy that God delights in is not only God's joy but also the joy of relative beings. Therefore, the joy of God as the subject must be the joy of Adam and Eve. In other words, God's joy becomes Adam's joy, God's joy becomes Eve's joy, Adam's joy becomes Eve's joy, Eve's joy becomes Adam's joy, and the joy of Adam and Eve becomes God's joy; this is truly a unified joy. The place where human beings and God can have a love that is complete without any deficiency or bias is the position of a mature couple receiving love. However, Adam and Eve did not see such a beginning. We know that this is the result brought about by the fall.

Moreover, because they did not receive perfect love as parents, even if those parents give birth to children, they cannot express perfect love as parents. If those parents had experienced perfect love, they would be able to give perfect love to their children. If they give birth and love their children from a position of not having experienced perfect love, that love is only the love below what they have experienced, not above it. From this perspective, has God, as the true parent who has not fallen, ever loved a child whom He could love? He has not.

The reason God created humans
Today, we speak of parental love even in this fallen world. We know that fallen parents love their children even at the cost of their lives. When we see that those parents, connected by fallen love, sacrifice their lives to love their children, how strong would the heart of a parent who gave birth to a child after receiving God's perfect love as a perfect child, perfect couple, and perfect parent be? Since that is the standard of perfection, it would be the strongest love imaginable.

God cannot push that love away. Before that love, God sheds tears, and without that love, He can only feel sadness, so even the absolute being can be governed by that love.

Happiness is achieved through relative conditions. Happiness devoid of emotional aspects cannot exist. Happiness connects the emotional foundation established by perfect relative conditions, and when relative conditions are not met, it is lonely. In loneliness, there can be no satisfaction or hope.

When we consider this, if humans had established a relationship of children centered on God's perfect love, how amazing would that history have been? If that had happened, standing in a vertical position and connecting with God centered on absolute love would have been a given, but that vertical love would also connect horizontally to their descendants, meaning that just as God loves Adam and Eve, Adam and Eve would stand in a position aligned with God's love and be able to love their children in the same way. If that were the case, the position regarding those children would also have to align with God, and we must understand this here. Therefore, God's love ultimately flows to the children through Adam and Eve.

The love of those children does not end with the love of the children. Because that love is connected through the parents, if it becomes a foundation to return to the parents, it becomes the ideal realm of love centered on the Unification Church, the realm of the son-in-law.

Then, if God exists, does He need people? Yes, He does need people. Who created people? God created them. While God needs people, He is the subject who has the ability to create people endlessly. From this, we can understand that God does not need people themselves. He can create them. Then, does He need material? Material is also created by God.

So why does He need people? He does not need people themselves, but He needs them to have a target for love; that is the only purpose for which He needs them. Does God need material? Does He need power? He does not need any of those things. He possesses everything. Since God is absolute, there is no being in the world that can surpass His authority. Since God created everything, what is needed does not exist in the realm of existence. What God needs is neither power nor money. What knowledge does God need? He does not need knowledge either.

Then why did He create people? It was not to see the form of people. What is so wonderful about seeing people? When you look at a face, it can seem strange. You might think, "Why do they look like that?" If you think about it, you cannot be driven mad or love them just by seeing them. He did not create people because He liked their appearance.

So why did He create them? He created them to have a counterpart within Himself to act and feel stimulation. He already possesses everything else. What is that? It is because He needs the substance of a target that can evoke the feeling of love. That is how it is. If there is beauty within God, He possesses it to such an extent that there is no greater beauty. To reflect such introspective qualities onto a counterpart and to form a broad atmosphere of love through the reactions that arise from those stimuli, He created people.

Therefore, even if a parent loves a child from afar, separated to the ends of the earth, it is not a separation. The farther apart they are, the more that love does not diminish. Truly loving individuals desire to be closer the more they are separated. Is that not so? In the world of love, distance can be transcended. Outside of that, it cannot be.

Then, what is the essence that allows the infinite God, the infinite being, to govern His infinite authority? It is not ability. Authority cannot surpass its own limits. What can surpass those limits? Only the power of love can do that. The essence that can manage the infinite world and the eternal world is not authority or knowledge. It must be the power of love. We cannot help but think this way. When we see this, we understand that God created humans because He needs objective love.

The essence that can govern the infinite authority is love.
Then how does love manifest? Does it first manifest as the love of the people? No, it does not manifest first as the love of the people. It does not first manifest as brotherly love either. When we pursue the path of how love manifests, the very first path of love's manifestation is that if God is truly the subject of love... What is the best thing in the human world? It is parental love. That is how it is.

In establishing the tradition of true love, what tradition must the absolute God first establish? He must first establish the tradition of parental love. For this reason, God cannot help but be a father. God is a Father. He must inherit the tradition of loving the Son to see the beginning of true love. He must have wished for parents to completely love their children and for children, that is, sons and daughters, to establish a perfect relationship of love. That is how it is.

Then what comes next? After that is established, the love of couples must be formed. After that, those couples must have the right to rejoice like God and resemble God. Just as God possesses parental love, child love, and couple love, and loves their children, they too must embrace their children in love. Here, they will establish a path and develop horizontally. This is beyond question.

For this reason, fathers must express perfect love. God also wishes for sons and daughters who receive perfect love to achieve love as perfect couples. After establishing the love of couples, they must achieve love as parents. That is, just as God loves Adam and Eve, those humans must also wish to love their children from the same position. Shouldn't this be the point of intersection? Here, it is finally the same. That is, the vertical and horizontal are the same. Shouldn't it be hoped that this would happen?

If that were the case, where would happiness exist in the world? Happiness does not exist in the future world apart from humanity. Where is happiness? It is in the place from which one has started. Therefore, history should not be about searching for happiness but about following happiness... History should be about aligning with the standard of happiness, yet today we have lost that standard of principle and have become humans pursuing future happiness.

Complete restoration is achieved centered on love.
If humans were originally such beings, they would have become miserable. Because they have entered the realm of the fate of the fall, they have fallen into a position where they should not be. At some point, they must extract and re-present the standard of truth so that humanity can finally find the standard of original hope, the standard of happiness, and the standard of ideals. In other words, they must restore it.

So when is complete restoration achieved? Complete restoration is achieved at the end of the historical age. What is the end? It is the time to find the lost standard of perfect ideal love. If that standard is sown and planted, and through a process, results are achieved, then at any time, it will stand in an objective position before God. However, because that has not happened, we are looking forward to the time and place where it can be unified. Only when that time comes can God finally see completion, and when God sees completion, humanity can also finally see completion. That standard can be the standard of perfection for fallen humans, those who have fallen. This cannot be anything but God's fulfillment of hope. That standard must emerge. To re-present that standard, God is coming forth with hope for humanity. There can be nothing else.

When that standard is not attained, God's will cannot be fulfilled. As long as we humans do not reach that standard of ideal love, we cannot re-present the fundamental standard. If that is not possible, humanity will end in misery in a miserable world. However, if that is possible, humanity may have started in misery but can end in happiness.

Because there is an absolute God, originally, humans were born as God's sons and daughters, but that one and only son and daughter have died. It is the heart of the parents that wishes to revive the dead sons and daughters, and for this reason, the parent God has been working to revive them. We must understand that this is the history of restoration.

Then, what is complete restoration centered on? It is centered on love. From love comes life, and from life comes hope... In that hope, we are living. Therefore, when we ask whether love comes first or life comes first, it is not life that comes first. Life begins from love. Why did God create humans? He did not create them to see the lives of His sons and daughters. He created humans to love them. No matter how you think about it, it must be so.

The purpose of creating humans is love. Life was created based on God's love, not the other way around, where life was created to evoke love. In other words, love began to sprout in God's heart, and life began from that love, so the result must also be love. Do you understand what I mean? Because the beginning was love, the end must also be love. Therefore, without love, we humans are unhappy.

So what is love? It is not about oneself. It is something that occurs in a relative relationship. Love occurs between two or more; it must happen in the relationship between subject and object.

Perfect love
So, why were we humans born? We were born for love. Is that not so? That is the truth. You must understand this clearly.

What is love? It is to fully value the object. One must stand in that position for love to be established. You must understand that. In establishing love, saying, "Ah, I exist to value myself," does not establish perfect love. Perfect love is established from a position that values others one hundred percent. That is the principle. Do you understand? Love is not established from a self-centered position. Perfect love begins from a position that can fully value the object. Humans were born with that purpose, and because they are in that position, they cannot deny it.

Why is that? For whom were men and women born? For whom was a man born? Did a man born for another man? Did a man born for himself? Why did Kim, who is overweight, come into existence? For a woman? "Yes." Did he come into existence for that? That sounds unpleasant, doesn't it? A man was not born for another man. For whom was he born? For someone absolute, for someone else.
"Because of women." Is that really true, Mr. Kim? How long have you thought about it? 
This is the problem. Men were absolutely born for women. This is 
a very obvious fact, yet they do not understand it.
"There is love on the path of men." They think it is their love. That 
is madness. This must be clearly understood. A man who thinks he was born because of himself will disappear even if he lives a hundred years. 
He won't last even a century. Once he dies, that's it. However, a person who says, "I was born for women," still has hope. 
That is how it is. 
Then, for whom are women born? Were women born for themselves? For whom were they born? Here, grandmothers, for whom were you born? They were born for men. If they were born with the idea of living for themselves, there is no love or anything else. They were born for life, but when we pursue our essential life, did they come for themselves? 
They were born for others. This must be clearly understood. From this perspective, we cannot deny that humanity started with love at its center.
Love is completely about serving others. It is in the fact that they were born for others that love is established; if they were born for themselves, there is no love or anything else. 
In a loving couple, love is established in their mutual care for each other; does love establish itself in saying, "You must do this for me"? That is temporary. That is love that adjusts to the feelings of the other, and it cannot be true love. From this perspective, humanity was born for the ideal of love. 
Why is serving others good? When fathers or mothers or schools educate, they all say, "You should do good deeds." What is a good deed? Is it good to go out and knock someone down with your fist? 
It is to sacrifice oneself for others. To sacrifice means to expend oneself, to give to others... A good person or a virtuous person is someone who sacrifices themselves.
What happens to a person who sacrifices? They become a subject that can evoke love. This must be understood. Right?
A person who sacrifices for their country can evoke love for the country, a person who sacrifices for their family can evoke love for the family, and a person who sacrifices for their comrades can evoke love for their comrades. You must understand this. Therefore, even if we humans do not know it, sacrificing for others is good.
What does religion teach? It teaches God's love and has the mission to achieve the purpose of God's love, so religion teaches sacrifice. That is natural. If religion tries to dominate the world centered on itself, it cannot be. Do you understand what I mean?
The Unification Church teaches sacrifice. The members of the Unification Church are all told to sacrifice for a nation greater than the Unification Church. If they sacrifice for the country with a heart of sacrifice that has not appeared in this country or this nation until now, then a spirit of patriotism that has not appeared in history will manifest here. Do you understand? When a new tradition of loving the people is established here, the organization that establishes that tradition will not perish. That is theoretical. It is not blind. Do you understand? Today, the Unification Church is working to embrace the nation completely and to have that nation sacrifice for the world.
Then what will happen to that nation? It will establish a new, higher tradition of love for the world in front of all humanity, not just patriotism but a world love based on philanthropy. Therefore, once that is planted, all people will love that path of love. They would have loved it in the past, they love it now, and they will love it in the future. There is no temporal or conceptual aspect that surpasses this. Everything will standardize and come to a conclusion based on this. 
This is the origin and source, so that love is what humanity needs.
Pursuing a world of peace centered on that love is the principle, so the thought of the Unification Church teaches that on the day the Republic of Korea is restored, it will bind the people of the Republic of Korea and teach them to sacrifice for all humanity. This is the nation the Unification Church seeks. Is that good or bad? "It's good."
If that happens, will it perish? Even if it is told to perish, it will not perish. Why will it not perish? Because God is extremely pleased. Where God is pleased, there is no one to strike. If God dislikes something, Satan may come and attack, and there may be invasions by evil, but if someone invades where God is extremely pleased, there is no forgiveness.
What is the struggle between evil spirits and good spirits centered on? You must understand that it is centered on love. Ultimately, when one sacrifices for a greater cause, on the day they go with a heart of love to sacrifice, it is managed by good spirits; conversely, a person who loves themselves and sacrifices others is managed by evil spirits. This is how it is clearly divided. 
Today, people cannot distinguish this. If one says, "I was born for myself, and you were born for me," they are a goblin. They are a daytime goblin. When the leaders of the Republic of Korea fight among themselves, they are nothing more than daytime goblins. We must discern these things and organize them well. Do you understand?
Originally, humans were born to serve others. They were born to sacrifice for others. 
What happens when one sacrifices for others? Not only is the tradition of love established, but they become the center of love. What do they become? They undoubtedly become the center of love.
In a school, it is like the person who works for the entire class becoming the class president. A person who stands in a position of serving others while being in the same place becomes the class president. If someone loves the Republic of Korea more than anyone else, has lived for the Republic of Korea more than anyone else, and is living for the Republic of Korea more than anyone else, then they naturally become a national center. That is how it is. 
That cannot be denied.
What will a person who becomes the center of love do? They will rise to the top. The center rises to the top. When they reach the top, they can automatically lead and manage the group. They become the overseer. This is the principle of heaven. This must be clearly understood.
What is an evil person? An evil person is someone who says, "You exist for me." The communist way is, "What is yours is mine, and what is mine is mine." That may prosper temporarily. They may rise, but they will eventually fall. However, goodness does not fall; when it rises, it continues to rise. It does not fall but continues to rise. How far will it rise? It will rise to the position of dominating the world, a position that can even subjugate God. It will rise to the position that desires even God. Therefore, those who live for others prosper, while those who live for themselves perish. 
Where does the start of complete restoration begin? 
Where does human perfection begin? It starts from oneself. How can perfection exist? It can exist centered on love. Is that not so? Would you prefer perfection centered on money or perfection centered on love? Answer me. Would you prefer perfection centered on money or perfection centered on love? Or would you prefer perfection centered on knowledge or perfection centered on love? There is no need to ask. No matter how fallen a human may think with an ignorant brain, they will inevitably pursue perfection centered on love. 
Where is the standard of perfection that can start centered on love? It is me, me. What is the position of "I"? Originally, it was born to serve others. Is that not so? What is the position of serving others? "It is a perfect position." It is a perfect position.
If one must live for others, they have thought of it negatively. However, the highest perfect position is the position that starts from serving others. Then, what kind of person can achieve restoration and completion? It is a person who has lived madly for others. That is the conclusion.
How is God now? Because God is perfect, He has existed for others until now. However, since there has not yet been a counterpart that has reached the absolute standard, He is working until the counterpart reaches the absolute standard. That is the only conclusion that can be drawn. You must understand that.
Where will complete restoration start? From a position centered on oneself? No. It starts from a position that completely denies oneself. This may feel unpleasant, but it cannot be helped. That is why someone like Jesus is truly a great person. When we look at what he said, "Those who wish to die?" "Live." "Those who wish to live?" "Die." When we see this, we recognize the greatness of Jesus and the greatness of the Bible. It fits perfectly.

So does this mean we should live only for the Republic of Korea? No, it does not mean living only for the Republic of Korea. The Republic of Korea must live to become a nation that can inherit the world. Therefore, it is not this country. It is not a country like this. A new nation must be created. We are pursuing a nation that countless countries in the world can look up to and welcome day and night. It must be a nation that God can welcome as well. 
A true path is one that teaches us to pursue a nation that was the embodiment of hope in the past world, can be said to be the center of ideals in the present world, and can be called an eternal starting point that we can inherit in the future world. If it is not such a religion, it cannot break through to the ultimate victory point. You must understand this. 
Who do you live for? If you say, "I live for myself," that is a failure. Can there be a family for someone who lives for themselves? There is no hopeful family. Can there be a nation? A nation cannot emerge. Can there be a world? There cannot be a world. There is no place for the world to emerge. Is there or isn't there? The covenant of heaven and earth is to say, "Get away, you individualistic villain," and to stop it. Can a family enter where individualism is prioritized? Can any ideal nation enter there? Can it fit into a place as narrow as the tip of a needle? No matter how hard you try to enter, you cannot. 
Therefore, the ideology of the Unification Church is to live for the world rather than for the Republic of Korea, not only now but also for the past and the future. It is different from the world. Who should we live for? If the scope of living for others is large, can a family that lives for others enter there? Yes, it can. Can a nation that lives for others enter there? Yes, it can. Can a world that lives for others enter there? Yes, it can. It is bound to enter. Therefore, we are told to live for others. 
A good person is not someone who causes harm but someone who suffers harm. Right? There are no good people among those who cause harm. A person who suffers harm is a good person. Think about it. That is undoubtedly true. Parents tell children that if they go out and fight with other children morning and night, they will become bad kids, right? 
But if you give benefit rather than cause harm, what is that? Is it evil or good? It is good. Good people are bound to give benefits. Is that for their own benefit? It is for the benefit of the other. It is living for others. Then why is this good? Is it true that an ideal family cannot arise from this? Yes, it can. Is it true that an ideal society cannot arise? Yes, it can. It can. An ideal nation and an ideal world can emerge from there. Where the ideal type appears becomes the foundation that God can expect, so those who stand in such a place receive blessings. Even if they say they do not want to, they receive them. This is the strategy we should pursue. 
If this fails, history has nowhere to go. People like Jesus become the lowest of the low. They become the lowest of the low among the followers. They might seem to end there and disappear without a trace, but because God exists… The dead Jesus did not die for Himself. He died for all people, which makes Him a great man. 
Therefore, the Unification Church should not become a church that moves only for itself. 
What are we doing now? We are working to save the nation. After working to save the nation, does the Unification Church fail? Right now, the Unification Church itself is at a minus. If we reflect on ourselves, we have not worked for the Unification Church at all. Then can the Unification Church fail? It cannot fail. Can it fail? No. You must understand this. 
Now, if we stop focusing on the Republic of Korea and live for the world, and if we live until the people of the world recognize us, then the world will be led by those who live for the world. Therefore, if the world is led, it becomes the subject of the world and the center of the earth. Since God comes to this world to find a center, if it becomes the center of the earth, He cannot help but come here. That is the fastest way in the world. That individual is the center of the family and the center of the ethnicity. That individual is the center of the nation and the center of the world. The one who comes to fulfill such a mission on earth is the Messiah. 
So how will the Messiah come? If He comes with only a personal foundation, He can only be a personal subject. Right? A man alone cannot be a subject. If this is a vertical subject, there is only a vertical standard, so a horizontal standard is needed. Without the combination of vertical and horizontal, harmony cannot occur. The cross is the combination of vertical and horizontal. Right? It combines vertical and horizontal in all directions. 
A world representative nation that can stand above communist countries. 
Therefore, if the Messiah who comes to this earth, if Jesus is indeed the Messiah of humanity, what does He come to find? Since Jesus is a man, it is natural for Him to seek a bride. Thus, He forms a family. This family is not just for His own family or for His own ethnicity. It is a family that represents the family of the world. When a family that represents the global family comes together to form a clan, that clan becomes a clan for the world, not just for a specific ethnicity. When that clan comes together to form a nation, that nation becomes a nation that can inherit the world, not just a nation for a specific country. That nation must form a state. That state emerges as a nation that represents the world, not just for a specific country. This is the ideal nation. 
There should be no obstacles in going from the individual to the family, clan, ethnicity, nation, and world. The victory point must be passed from the individual to the family, from the family to the ethnicity.
We must inherit this victory point. In such a pattern, the victory points of families should be inherited by tribes, the victory points of tribes by nations, the victory points of nations by the world. This pattern must be able to be passed down consistently from individuals to the world without change from the moment of its inception. Unless a foundation with a consistent connection is established on earth, the providential final victory that God desires cannot be manifested on this land. Without such a foundation, a world of peace cannot come to this earth. There can be no hope. You must understand this.

Our Unification Church is an organization that has appeared to awaken individuals to such hope. We are not only called to be individuals but also to establish such families. We must not only focus on families but also organize a new tribe. This tribe must transcend national sentiments to form a global tribe. In this sense, the Unification Church has gathered the peoples of ten nations to hold a joint marriage ceremony.

They are not children of their respective countries. They are a global group formed to establish families that can inherit new victory points centered on a new ideal. By organizing a tribe that transcends nations and national sentiments, and by expanding its numbers, a nation that can stand above any country in this evil satanic world, a sovereign nation that God can be proud of, will be formed. On that day, a foundation will be established on earth that can represent the omnipotent power of God before Satan. At that time, the era of judgment will come. A subjective era will come that governs the world centered on absolute law. It can be concluded that that time will be the era of earthly judgment.

For this reason, God is not seeking nations but is seeking a nation. Even if Satan has created an evil world with dozens or hundreds of countries, there is only one country among them that can be proud. Even if there are hundreds of marathon runners, there is only one person who can be proud of being first. Similarly, in the evil world, the representative country that Satan can boast of before God and can drive God into suffering is the one country that is most loyal to Satan. In other words, among many satanic countries, it is principled to pursue evil centered on one representative country. Therefore, when a good country emerges that can stand above one of these evil satanic countries, it can boldly smash the satanic world. This has not been understood until now. Christianity has not known this.

Today, the Communist Party represents the satanic world. Therefore, centered on the Lord who comes from the democratic world today, we must establish a sovereign nation that surpasses the sovereign nations of the communist world. In the communist world, life is threatened and coerced, creating a situation of life or death, but the Lord who comes does not bring such an ideology. Rather than being threatened by others and sacrificing one's life, He seeks to create a sovereign nation formed by those who willingly sacrifice their lives. Thus, when that nation can stand above the nations of the communist world, united as one with the sovereign and the people, on that day, it will be possible to strike down the Communist Party as long as God is present. When Kim Il-sung is called away and Mao Zedong is called away, and the third generation is replaced, that is the day of destruction. You must understand that.

Then, what is the purpose for which we are called today? For a nation that God can find and rule the world, for a more valuable nation... To become a nation and people that can stand above any nation in history and boast of a historical tradition while serving one sovereign is the mission of Christianity and the mission of many religions.

Who is the sovereign who comes? He is the Messiah. The Messiah does not come to lead individuals. The Messiah comes to govern nations and peoples. Yet, because there is no foundation for individuals, we must pave the way for individuals, and because there is no foundation for families, we must pave the way for families, and because there is no foundation for tribes, nations, and countries, we must pave those paths.

Why is that? Because the Israelite people and Judaism could not unite and pave that foundation, the basis for Jesus to govern a nation was broken. Jesus, who did not have such a national foundation, unfortunately did not have a familial foundation, nor did He have an individual foundation. Since the family is the origin of forming a nation, Jesus, who could not find a family, left the last will saying, "I will die but will come back to find a family," which is the ideology of the bride and bridegroom of Christianity. Thus, it can be said that Jesus did not even start. It is tragic. Jesus left without being able to fulfill His role as a man.

If Jesus had a family and direct descendants, under whose governance would Christianity be today? It would be governed by the good direct descendants of Jesus, and there could not be a Pope like Paul VI. There could not be Presbyterians, Methodists, or any division between old and new churches. A systematic global sovereign nation would have been automatically formed, and had such a foundation existed, communism could not have emerged.

The reason for this tragic outcome is that Jesus' death became the motivation, and because of Jesus' death, this historical misfortune came to be, something that Christian believers cannot even dream of. To resolve this misfortune, a new nation and world must be formed. A nation that pledges its origin to individuals, families, tribes, peoples, and nations will dominate the world. A nation that lives like this will not perish. If such a nation perishes, God will perish. God can only fulfill His will by supporting and developing such a group. When such groups are removed, God cannot exist. As long as God exists, such a group will remain.

Therefore, the final point of victory is something you must pave. Where should that foundation go? Individuals must pass it on to families, families to tribes, and tribes to nations. When a nation receives this, what must happen? A new exodus of Israel must unfold. Do you understand? In this way, when that nation becomes a people that can inherit a new world on a national scale, it will represent the world and govern the world.

The thought of the Unification Church is to create such a nation through Korea. You must understand this. We must completely inherit this from Korea to the world, from the spiritual realm to the physical realm. Only when this is united before God can the point of peace, which determines God's love, be formed in this universe, and only then will the final victory point be established in heaven and earth.

Then God can finally smile and say, "Ah! It is all accomplished!" and "Before me, there is only happiness. There will no longer be a historical path of grievance, resentment, and sacrifice." This must be stamped. We must have a day when the spirits in this earthly realm and the spiritual realm are liberated, and they can praise victory from a completely liberated position. Only then will the final victory point be determined. You must understand that we must overcome this to enter the eternal era of the kingdom of peace in heaven and earth, where true happiness begins. We must go for that. I was born for that...

In a way, we have nothing. Even if we look at Reverend Moon of the Unification Church, he has nothing. It seems like there is a church and everything, but everything he has is for others and for the world. Just because I have money does not mean I think of buying a suit or a house. Even though I live in this house now, if I had money, I would want to use it for the country.

This time, I traveled abroad and spent hundreds of thousands of dollars. How great it would have been if I had spent that money for Korea. Right? The Unification Church in Korea is struggling. Even now, if you go to the countryside, there are churches that look like goblin houses. But do not be ashamed of that. Do you understand?

A farmer who sleeps in the wilderness and sows seeds with life in his hands is engaging in a futile and pitiful game. Is he foolish for sowing even a measure of seed? If he sows without knowing the result, he is extremely foolish. It is exactly the same. Despite the difficulties of the Unification Church, we are sowing money for the world. Among the people of the Republic of Korea, there are those who criticize this. There are rumors about how Reverend Moon of the Unification Church spends a hundred thousand dollars and how much money he spends.

Why do we do this? To perish? Just like a farmer who sows only a measure of seed, even with that little, we are sowing for the world. So, after sowing, do we get chased away? No. When the time comes for me to be chased away, the people of the world will say they will be chased away instead of me, and on that day, the world will exist for the Unification Church. Why? Because the Unification Church exists for the world, the world must exist for the Unification Church. This is the natural principle.

Therefore, we must live for this. If someone feels sad about their shabby clothes, they must perish. They must perish. If someone sheds tears over the pitiful reality they face, they must perish. The teacher has transcended such notions. If one feels resentful about a shabby place to lie down and thinks about the past, they will perish. Who looks at the Unification Church itself and says, "Why is the Unification Church headquarters like this?" or "What is Reverend Moon like?" or "Since it has become something global, shouldn't we build a new headquarters?" I know all too well. However, we must continue until the end, until we reach the world. If the Unification Church fails despite doing so, then Reverend Moon of the Unification Church is a fake.

However, Reverend Moon of the Unification Church has not failed. I have nothing, but wherever I go, I have a place to stay. Wherever I go, I have a foundation that is not inferior to anyone. Even if I do not want it, they want to give me the best car in that country. Why is that? Because the subject and object of giving and receiving... the object must appear as a relative value corresponding to the driving force of the subject. When the counterpart cannot reach the standard of the subject, it is the principle of heaven that they feel sorry and want to stand before proportional standards. Even if humanity has fallen, it is because of this nature that restoration is possible.

Foreign members are doing well for the teacher, yet they are still cautious. They wonder what the teacher thinks... It is not because they fear the teacher, but because their true heart is like that. That is the principle. When you see your true heart like that, you must understand that such a path cannot fail.

The ideal of our Unification Church is to liberate even hell. Do you understand now? We aim to liberate even hell. Liberation comes simply by listening to the teacher's words.

In this sense, the ideal owner, God, is not someone who creates hell to give humans pain and takes joy in it. Humans are the sons and daughters of God. When the day of joy comes, when it becomes a festive day, even the passing beggar, even the unrelated beggar, must be made happy; that is the principle. Therefore, you must clearly understand that God is not someone who wants to keep humanity, which is in a position similar to that of His children, in such a groaning place while only God reigns as the eternal king of peace.

When the standard is established that anyone from any nation can receive God's love, we will finally reach the destination of victory, and we must run toward that place. Where do you stand? If you live for yourself, you will have no choice but to live that way even in the spiritual realm later. They will not have a family. They cannot have an ideal family. They cannot form connections within an ideal tribal realm. It is lonely. It should not be that way, should it? But that is how it will be.

Today, if our hearts share a common ideal with all of humanity and we say we want to live like brothers, we must devote ourselves wholeheartedly to that. If we desire that and wish to love like that, and if we can run joyfully day and night, then there will be no stage that is blocked when we go to the spiritual realm.

From that perspective, when members of our Unification Church pray, "Please fulfill the global purpose. Have they thought even a little about their nephews or nieces? Ladies! Have you thought even a little about your cousins? It is all wrong.

When the time comes, you should say, "Ah, our ideal time has come. The time has come when the people of the Republic of Korea can love the people of the world, a first in the historical era." With all your sincerity, even offering a piece of biscuit would be fine. Even a sip of barley tea would be good. Only by moving to establish a relationship with them, even with a single condition, can you occupy the position of a proactive Unification Church member in the future. If foreign members put in more sincerity than you do, then you must pass that position on. Should you pass it on or not? If God is present, should you pass it on or not? Answer me. Should you pass it on or not? "Ah, since the Unification Church came from Korea, we cannot leave out Korea." Can you say that? Absolutely not. Water flows from high places to low places, so when a path opens in a lower place, does it not flow down the lower path, leaving the higher path behind? "It flows." That is the same principle.

Among the members of the Unification Church scattered around the world, who loves the world more? When I quietly observe you, you do not even think about how the church is running or what is happening. God is not just the God of the Republic of Korea. God is not just the God of the Unification Church in Korea. God is the God of the Unification Church members of the world.
The teacher was born in the Republic of Korea. When I think about it, it is astonishing that I was born in the Republic of Korea. After working, you must feel ashamed before heaven, realizing that there are still responsibilities left for us to fulfill, and you must walk the path where you can shed tears for not being able to do more. Endure and overcome. Fight until the end for the hope of tomorrow."

Our Path
If there is a person who acts based on the standard of these principles, the power of the universe must be responsible for creating an object before such a person. Therefore, those around them will automatically know that they should pursue such a person and should not be separated from them. If there are five people around, they will not separate from each other even after a year. As time goes on, they will say, "If you are in a place where you will die, I will die in your place." This is how it changes. As time goes on, rather than separating, they become more united around the center. You must understand that this is the turning point between good and evil.

Humanity does not know the path of good.
However, when we look at the world today, there is no center in this world. Humanity does not know where the center is that they must go to. They cannot distinguish between what is good and what is evil. They do not know what the path of good is for individuals, families, nations, and the world.

* This message was given at the first national mobilization evangelism training session, and the earlier part is not recorded.
This universe has directions: east, west, south, and north. Similarly, heavenly fortune moves along the seasons just like these directions. Therefore, there are nations corresponding to the fortunes of the eastern season, as well as nations corresponding to the fortunes of the western season, and there are nations experiencing prosperity like the south, while others are in a state of freezing like the north.

Humans do not understand this. Therefore, it must be emotion (情), knowledge (知), and will (意). But it is reversed. 
Raise your hand if you say, “I like knowledgeable people.” Raise your hand if you say, “I like my mother because she is the president of Ewha Womans University.” If there is someone who likes that, raise your hand. That is how it should be. “I like them because they have knowledge.” A person who says that is a crazy person.

The current situation of the Republic of Korea and the purpose of the emergence of the Unification Church

You must understand how urgent the situation is for our Republic of Korea right now. If there were time, I would talk about it, but I will stop because there is no time. Look. Our Republic of Korea is in an extremely unjust position.

Originally, our Republic of Korea has been recognized as a single nation in the world since December 12, 1948, when it received sovereignty from the UN General Assembly. North Korea is an exception. It is condemned as an invader. It cannot be recognized as a legitimate entity on the Korean Peninsula. Yet, the reality that more and more countries in the world sympathize with North Korea is an extremely unjust fact. The Republic of Korea started well, but why did it fall into a position where it could not receive support from the UN along the way? Of course, Korea itself is miserable, but we must also observe that the world situation is entering a miserable abyss.

However, even if the world is going that way and the situation in our Republic of Korea is turning that way, if we have a sense of national pride based on justice, we must step over any obstacles and continue to run toward the good ideology we originally started with, centered on the purpose of unification. When we push forward with the spirit of perseverance, we can bring about unification, but if we become a nation that thinks appropriately from the perspective of considering our own misfortunes and following the environment or looking around, we will not find the Republic of Korea that is the desired nation, nor the desired nation that the UN hopes for. If that happens, it would be better if the North and South had not been divided at all. Isn't that right? Isn't it so? It all becomes like that.

In light of this, why has our Unification Church emerged today? The purpose of the Unification Church's emergence is not only the unification of the Republic of Korea but also to create one Asia, not only Asia but one world, not only the world but also to unify the spiritual world, and not only the spiritual world but also to unify the spiritual and physical worlds to become one with God, and not only to become one with God but ultimately to unify centered on God's love. This is the tremendous task for which the Unification Church has started.

To put it another way, do you know the stork? How does a stork look? It looks similar to a crane, right? There is such a stork. There is also a smaller bird called a "jjaksae." Do you know what a "jjaksae" is? When you go to a rice paddy, there is a small bird that is much smaller than a stork. Some of you may not know it well. If you look, the stork and the crane look similar. And the jjaksae also looks similar to the stork. However, no matter how much the jjaksae tries to follow the stork, it cannot catch up, and no matter how much the stork tries to follow the crane, it cannot catch up. Isn't that so?
