**Message**: All human beings living on this earth, regardless of who they are, face the daily life and look forward to the path of their lives. We know that in this life, good and evil are determined, and that the works of God and Satan are intertwined.

A life that aligns with the eternal purpose and direction of the will must be achieved. Therefore, how we leave behind good in our daily lives and how we eradicate evil in our individual lives is an important issue for those who practice faith.

When we speak of the path of the will, the will is not an abstract concept. It is a concrete will. If that will has a purpose, there must be a direction toward that purpose. No matter how much a purpose exists, if the direction does not align, that purpose becomes irrelevant to us. The farther away that purpose is, the more we must pay special attention to that direction.

If the purpose is close, it may be easy to align the direction, but the farther away the purpose is, the more difficult it becomes to align the direction to achieve that purpose. If the purpose is visible before our eyes, we may rush toward it without considering the direction, but the farther away the purpose is, the more ambiguous the direction becomes.

God's will includes personal will, family will, national will, global will, and ultimately the will of the heavenly sovereignty that our Unification Church speaks of. If God is centered on the will for heaven and earth to become one, then we humans must not deviate from that purpose. Moreover, we must understand that it is impossible to reach the desired destination of God unless the direction we are heading aligns with the direction God is heading.

The question of whether an individual succeeds on this earth or whether they can leave behind a day-to-day life that achieves their intended goals lies in how they establish a clear perspective centered on that purpose and how they can align their direction to match that purpose.

No matter how much one sets out with a common purpose, if the direction is misaligned, it becomes irrelevant to that purpose. Therefore, whenever we set out with a purpose, we must always pay attention to the issue of direction alignment.

When considering this direction alignment, I must stand in a straight line with the purpose. Since the relationship between the purpose and myself is always relative, I must stand in a position where I align with the purpose in a straight line. In our daily lives, when we move our right foot and then our left foot, if we do not take a position that aligns straight with the purpose, we will inevitably diverge. If we take even one wrong step, we will find ourselves misaligned. We must not lean to the right or to the left.

That is why we must find ourselves in a position that can harmonize with the purpose along the straight line drawn, and only then can we achieve the results of that purpose. If we disregard that straight line and stand on a temporal expectation that does not align with it, we must understand that the path to achieving the purpose has already gone off track.

Whether we speak or perceive through our senses, we must not feel alone. We cannot stand in a position where we feel alone. When we feel from a position that has a direction aligned with the purpose, that position is one that takes a collective stance toward a common purpose, and thus, God cannot help but be with us. If we diverge, God cannot accompany us.

Why is that? Because if the direction is wrong, all our efforts will return to nothing. If we cooperate, it does not bring mutual benefit; rather, it leads to mutual depletion. It becomes futile, and when we stand in such a position, it is only natural that God cannot cooperate or be with us.

From the moment we wake up in the morning, every sensation or action we feel must always align with a single purpose in a straight line. When we lose that point, we cannot establish a relationship with the will.
it becomes a different direction. 

This is countless. A day has 24 hours, and if you cut it in half, it becomes day and night. If you cut that day and night in half again, it becomes morning, afternoon, evening, and night. Night, centered around midnight, can also be divided into night and dawn. When you look at a day, you see that there is morning, afternoon, and evening. Although a day is small, it is similar to dividing the four seasons. Morning is like spring, afternoon is like summer, evening is like autumn, and night is like winter. If you break this down further, even within one hour, there are beginnings, processes, endpoints, and then the successes and failures of desires.

Faithful individuals should prioritize living each day correctly. If everything is interconnected in this way, isn't our human life in the same position? There is childhood, adolescence, youth, middle age, and old age. Regardless of size, we go through such processes in form.

When we talk about life, we refer to a lifetime. Life refers to something long. It describes the process from birth through childhood, youth, middle age, and into old age, meaning from birth until fate. That process is connected through living. Living refers to how we go about our daily lives.

Therefore, when living is flawed, life will also yield flawed results. No matter how excellent a life one tries to leave behind, if the daily living is flawed, that life will inevitably reach flawed results; this is an unavoidable conclusion.

In light of this, what should a believer prioritize? Even if one vows to dedicate their life to God, the issue is not the vow itself but how correctly one has lived each day in dedication. It is undeniable that without prioritizing a daily life that can continue that foundation, a fulfilling life cannot emerge.

When viewed this way, we may start a day without much thought, but we must always consider whether this day aligns with the eternal purpose and direction we desire. An unexpected wrongful action can turn one into a rebel against the path of eternal purpose, and such occurrences can happen within the daily life. If we break this down further, even within one hour, the boundaries of such actions can shift, and that one hour, or even one minute, or one second, becomes crucial. If even one minute or one second goes wrong, this direction can diverge forever. When we consider the gravity of such issues, it becomes clear that we should prioritize one hour over one day, and one minute and one second over one hour.

We must think about the fact that such issues are at stake for us. As you know, a compass points north and south. No matter how much you turn it east or west, it still points north and south. Even if it is placed in a position due to external forces, when that force is removed, it will automatically point north and south. In other words, even if you turn it in the opposite direction, it does not comply; rather, there is always a force acting to return to its original direction. We are well aware of this.

Similarly, humans should be able to point in one direction like a compass centered on God. If that direction diverges, there must be something that indicates the difference. Just as when you turn a compass to the opposite direction, there is a force acting to return to its original position, we must have a conscience that points towards God, and if we are turned in the opposite direction, there must be something that makes us aware that our inner self is acting in opposition.

Without such an action, humans cannot align with God's will throughout their lives, nor can they fulfill that purpose. Such an action exists regardless of east, west, north, or south, and it exists in every person. What is that action? It is the action of conscience. Just as a compass made of purer magnetism points more accurately north and south, a person with a pure conscience will always align with that direction.

That is why everyone, regardless of who they are, must strive to live a life that can align their direction daily. Here, the environment of good and evil collides. There will be times when one leans to the left and times when one leans to the right. Just as if you slightly move the position of a compass, it will oscillate left and right to find the center and align with north and south, you too must always strive to draw a position that aligns with one purpose. When we consider that human life is in such a position, our days cannot be unimportant, nor can one hour be unimportant.

The boundary of a moment is not determined by a day or an hour. Rather, it is centered around a minute or a second where good and evil are judged. When we look at this issue, the value that allows us to feel a day as eternal exists within that day, and the ability to determine the content of an hour with the same value as a day exists within that hour, and an hour can also be determined by minutes and seconds. When we consider that such content exists in smaller moments, will God's will change? The will is eternal. God's will does not change. No matter how much humans change and how much the environment changes, God's will cannot change.

There are immutable purposes that individuals must follow, purposes that families must follow, purposes that the Republic of Korea must follow, and perhaps purposes that the 3.6 billion people of the world must collectively follow.

When we go to the eternal world and live eternally within God's will, it will not be done blindly, disorderly, or without direction, but rather it will begin from a life centered on some eternal purpose. When we think about such issues, we must realize how serious our daily lives are. Dying is decided in a moment, and living is also decided in a moment. The fact that humans are born and die occurs in a moment, and when we say that the fate of our lives is determined by an hour, a minute, a second, or a moment, we must understand that the very life we live each day is the most important.

My sorrow begins at this moment. It is not that I plan a day and then sorrow according to that plan. Of course, there may be reasons for sorrow, but the fact of being sad is concluded in a moment. Joy, too, will go through processes like morning, afternoon, evening, and night, but the point at which we can see the endpoint of that joy is also a moment. When we consider these issues, we must ensure that even a single breath and a single action align with purpose.

As you know, when you go to a shooting range, to hit a target, the end of the gun must align with the target. The front sight and the rear sight must align with the target. If there is even a slight misalignment, the bullet will stray in all directions. Hitting the center of a target that is not easily visible is extremely difficult. The distance at the shooting range is usually 10 meters, and even hitting the center point at that distance is not an easy task.

However, if we must aim at a target throughout our lives with eternity in mind, how difficult would that be? Rather than just difficult, it would be unimaginably hard. When launching a satellite toward the moon, it is shot in a direction different from the moon's position. This is necessary to hit the moving moon. It must be accurate in the moment. Calculating the distance and the speed at which the moon moves to align the direction is essential for landing on the moon. Reaching the moon is indeed a challenge.

Humans, too, are like bullets shot toward a single purpose throughout their lives. They are indeed going somewhere. They eat, sleep, and wake up, repeating their lives, but they are going toward something. So where are they going? That is the question. Where is today going? Where is tomorrow going? Where is this month going? Where will next month go? Where have the twelve months of the year, the 365 days, gone? When you reach the last day of the year and reflect, did the starting point and the endpoint align? Did the life I led align with the direction of that purpose? This is a serious issue.

Believers must align their direction with the starting point of purpose. 

What kind of place is the place where I was born? That is the question. Following the flow of history, my ancestors left a path centered on purpose; where is the place my ancestors gave birth to me? Some were born at the southernmost end, some at the easternmost end, some at the westernmost end, and some at the northernmost end. Did not everyone come into the world from different places?

While the appearances of humans may be similar, the paths they must take diverge in all directions. This is the game humanity has been playing until now. Many people have suggested directions saying, "You must go this way" or "You must have this kind of thought."

When we look at these things, we see that the direction humans want to go and the direction God wants to go centered on His will are different. In other words, if we consider a single line, there are countless variations. While the will goes this way, some people go this way, others go that way, and there are all sorts of people. Some align after going this far, while others align after going that far; it is a myriad of variations. Additionally, the starting points differ in east, west, south, and north. Some start here, some start there; they are all different.

In light of such circumstances, the starting point of God's will is undoubtedly a significant issue. From that starting point, what kind of line will you draw? One must not become a person who does not leave a life that aligns with that line. Such a person is unfortunate. Depending on the proportion that aligns with that direction, there will be differences centered on that line or centered on God's will.

No matter how much one claims to be unfair, when viewed from this principle, the very claim of unfairness may place one in an unfair position. The position deemed unfair may sometimes align with the direction of purpose.

That is why the path of life is not simple. One must correct that path. Originally, humans were born to walk that path correctly. Therefore, should not what we see also align with that path? Where is the focal point that should be seen?

Isn't the eye there to see the direction that can align with the purpose? That goes without saying. Then why do we have a nose? Isn't it to maintain a relative relationship with that straight line and lead the direction without losing it? Everything works that way. Why do we have a mouth? Isn't it to provide nutrition in the pursuit of that purpose? Then why do we go? Of course, we come and go to do something, but isn't it to leave footsteps that can align with the direction of that purpose? Did not all our senses and limbs come into being to point toward the result that can align with that straight line?

When my own self, which should be in that position, fails to align, no matter how precious or excellent I am, I will fall into worthlessness and ruin. Therefore, everything we say or do, even sleeping and waking, must be based on this one line.

If we were to graph our lives, all sorts of pictures would be drawn. Let’s say we graph your day. What did you do? Sometimes you meet friends, sometimes you meet someone else, sometimes you fight with someone, and if you graph these things, you would indeed be living while drawing the picture of all things. Moreover, isn't everything you see, hear, and feel throughout the day different? When we sum it all up, where is that direction heading? Humans easily forget that they are living a life that determines that direction. Do people today think, "I have moved this far to the left, so to go right, I need to turn at this angle"? They do not think so. Are we not trapped in the habitual notion that we started from a position aligned with the correct direction and are still going? That is the problem.

Like a compass, if we recognize how much our angle is off and can naturally adjust it, that is one thing, but if we cannot act, we must deliberately take action to align our direction. Isn't this the life of a believer living differently from others in this world?

Then what is God's will? What is the will? "What is the will? The will is the will..." This cannot be the case. Within the will, there must be a perfected individual. There must be a man and a woman who can align with the will. There must also be a family that can align with the will. This is beyond question. Where is the destination that family must reach? It is to find the nation. There must be a nation that can align with the will, right? And there must be a world that can align with the will.

In this human world, there must be not only a flat world but also a vertical line that can align with the will. A vertical line alone is not enough. There must be parallel lines that are at 90 degrees. In other words, there must be both a three-dimensional world and a flat, horizontal world. The three-dimensional world and the horizontal world must intersect, but there will be those who say, "I am fine" at 60 degrees. A 60-degree angle does not align with the four directions. Isn't that so? To align with east, west, north, and south, it must be 90 degrees. No matter how you align it, it must be 90 degrees. From a principled standpoint, a point from which you can draw a perpendicular line to the parallel line, a north-south line, must be at 90 degrees. It must be at 90 degrees. The only point where a vertical line can rest is one. There cannot be another point. If there is another point, it means the angle is different by 1 or 2 degrees. If the angle changes...
It is not vertical.  
In the Unification Church, it is referred to as "Heavenly Principle." What does this Heavenly Principle mean? It refers to the direction in which vertical and horizontal lines can align at a 90-degree angle. This is true regardless of day or night, past, present, or future. No matter when or where you align them, they can match at a 90-degree angle. However, when we consider whether we live such a life in our daily existence, it is undoubtedly a serious issue.  

When we think about meaning, there is a meaning in which individuals can dwell, a meaning in which families can dwell, a meaning in which nations can dwell, a meaning in which the world can dwell, and a meaning in which God and humanity want to dwell together. God is a vertical being, and humanity is a horizontal being, so the intersection of vertical and horizontal can coexist eternally at that point. There is no term for something that is laid down as a center. When we say center, it must be a vertical line. There is no center on a horizontal line. A point on a horizontal line is referred to as the center. A single point that occupies a place becomes the center point. Can there be two centers?  

If there is heaven and earth, then heaven and earth become an axis and converge at one point. There can only be one such point. This center is one above and one below, which is the principle. This is not two.  

An individual must stand at this one point. A family must stand at that one point. The only difference is the scope. The scope is different. There is an individual centered around one point, a family centered around one point, a nation centered around one point, and the world must be connected centered around one point. This center is eternally the same. Only then can everything be concentrated at that one point and stand. As you can see with a top, no matter how heavy the top is, once it starts spinning, it spins better than a lighter top.  

So is there a place on this earth where such an axis can stand? There is none. The place where an individual can stand in meaning, or the path an individual can take in meaning, the place where a family can stand in meaning, or the path a family can take in meaning, the place where a nation can stand in meaning, or the path a nation can take in meaning, the point where heaven and earth can align, where vertical and horizontal can converge at one point, where God's will can be fully realized and human will can be fully realized, is the place where God and humanity are united.  

There can be no ideal if God and humanity are separated. An ideal is not achieved alone. No matter how much I sit and say, "I am an ideal person," an ideal cannot occur alone. An ideal occurs in a relational context. Can joy be achieved alone? It does not work that way. If joy could be achieved alone, there would be no need for God to create heaven and earth. Joy must occur in a relational context, in other words, in the relationship between subject and object.  

An ideal is not achieved alone. It is achieved in the relationship between subject and object. It occurs in a relational context. Joy does not occur in a place where relative beings are misaligned. Joy occurs when they meet at the same point centered around one point. Isn't that right? The subject and object are like north and south. Why must it be good to meet at the center? Because only at the center can the vertical line align perfectly.  

Why do we look toward that place? Only by being present at that place can the center be determined and become ideal. Why is it ideal? If it starts to spin at a slight angle from the center (gesturing with hand), later it will spin at an angle that is more than double. The less angle there is, the more it spins like this. Isn't that so? The narrower the distance, the more it becomes the center. That is the point of alignment. All moving beings must move according to the center. Depending on the distance from the center, if the distance is far, it will fall quickly; if it is close, it will fall slowly. The farther away, the less it moves; even if it does move, it will fall after one or two spins.  

The place where an individual can stand centered on God's will is not elsewhere. That place is the vertical point, the center point, so the individual must stand at that center point. Although the teacher returned to the world on the third course, when leaving, I had to get approval from the Ministry of Culture. I had to attach the minister's stamp to the documents, but I couldn't, so I got caught. However, it was Sunday, and the Ministry of Culture was closed. So, it was a big problem. I thought everything was set, but then I got caught, which was a huge issue. Time was pressing. I felt that I had to leave today. I was feeling something. If I didn't leave today, it would be a problem. I was reporting that I had been caught. "I must go!" I said, and I started running around.

The person responsible for the passport and the section chief was supposed to work at the airport, but since it was Sunday, he didn't come in. Moreover, the section chief had promised to spend the day at Chuncheon Lake with his colleagues. But that morning, he woke up and felt he didn't want to go no matter what. You know, God is truly grateful. At such times, you say thank you. (Laughter) He is the person in charge, so he must go, but he couldn't bring himself to leave.

So he thought, "Whatever, I’ll just cover myself with a blanket and sleep." But unexpectedly, someone knocked on the door looking for the section chief. There were three keys to the passport office, and all the keys were with the section chief. Since he had the keys to the main gate, the office, and the railroad tracks, nothing could be done without him. So we went to find the section chief and desperately chased him down, and we barely managed to leave just 15 minutes before departure. At the airport, they wondered, "What kind of people are they that the section chief comes out to work even on his day off?" They opposed and fought against it, but what could they do? They just had to give in. They had to leave like that.

If we didn't leave that day, it would have been a problem. The same goes for this time. If you just sit and think about it, then go, prepare... it becomes a mess. Three days before, I didn't even dream of it. It must be done that day. Someone who communicates with the spirit world comes and reports, "If this day goes wrong, this will happen. How do you know so well, teacher?" How do I know so well? I know well because I was born for such things! (Laughter)

When I returned to the world, people said, "How nice it must be for the teacher to travel the world! It must be nice to take people here and there." Is it nice? It is truly a matter of life and death, fighting on the brink of life and death. It is living in a state of extreme tension. You must understand that.

If you ask for recognition of your efforts, it is unfilial. You might say, "We prayed for the teacher at the headquarters, so the teacher returned well..." Not at all. The teacher is not someone who depends on your prayers. In order to leave your sincerity and efforts to the nation and the world, you must establish the relationship between the subject and the object and pray to encompass that environmental sphere globally. I am not someone who lives or dies because of your prayers. I am someone who goes without depending on your prayers. That does not mean, "From today, you don't have to pray for the teacher." If you want to do that, then go ahead. (Laughter) You do not understand such things.

You are reluctant to throw away even a dirty rag, right? You will flip it over and smell it before throwing it away. Satan will not retreat easily. That is why there is a fierce struggle. Why is that? The authority of justice is something that is given by the providence of salvation, even if one does not seek it. Even if you sit still, there will be people set as sentinels who can see what is happening on the other side, even to the depths of your being. That is the ideal of the teacher.

Because this foundation is not established, I am now walking this path of suffering with great difficulty to lay this foundation. That time will come. Many people are calling to meet the teacher without your knowledge, and I have cut them all off. You must know that the era when Unification Church members could come and go freely is over. If you are careless, you will say, “Oh no! I didn’t expect this, I didn’t expect this!” That time will come. You must be sure of that and become wise.

A wise person is someone who knows the times. The wise person is the one who adjusts to the times, rather than just welcoming them. Do you understand?

What will the path be like if you betray the purpose? I believe in God. Even if someone like you flows away, it will not harm me. You will be the one who suffers. Just wait and see.” That is a serious matter.

In that sense, while the teacher may be a good person, I also know that he is a frightening person. I have often seen that when I unknowingly think, “What a bad guy,” and a word slips out, within six or seven months, chaos ensues. That is strange. When I think about such things, the teacher is indeed a good person, but he is also a frightening person.

How will you teach your children the heart and the path of the purpose? I know that it is difficult for me to be a father. How should a father treat his children? He must become a friend among friends. Then, even while playing with their friends, when the father appears, they will abandon all their friends and run to their father. And he must become the teacher among teachers. In terms of heart, he must always be the landlord, that is, the center.

I know that there are people among you who criticize, “The teacher is strange. He takes the children to factories.” They say that going to factories is like going out for fun. Many people do not realize that our factory will become a foundation that develops families, a higher level of foundation. That is why I try to do that as much as possible. “Our father is the best, even better than the president. Even if he abandons his beloved wife, he will not abandon his father.” That is how it should be.

Now, looking at our Yejin, she is as tall as her mother. I try to do that with the children as much as possible. But now that she has grown, it feels awkward for her and for me. (Laughter) I feel that. Until she matures, in those moments when she cannot sleep, she will feel the father coming to stroke her like this (gesturing). That is necessary. We must create this new emotional tradition. “The president of the world is not the issue; our father is the best.” That is how it should be. “It is not about the teacher; our father is the best. It is not about friends; our father is the best.” That is how it must be.

Today, our Hyojin is preparing and waiting to follow her father. She says that when her father comes, she will go somewhere with him, and when we go, she wants to ride in the Lincoln car. Sometimes she asks, “Could you take me to Gyeongju on Sunday?” I said, “What Gyeongju on Sunday? On Sunday, we are not supposed to go anywhere, so if we go, we can stop by on the condition that we go to Daegu, but we cannot just go.” Just going to Gyeongju is not allowed by my conscience. I do not know after we finish worship, though. Now, even our Gukjin is stepping up, saying he will follow his father. That is not a bad thing; the problem is that we cannot do that. Education is truly difficult. It is not easy to be a father.

All these issues revolve around one purpose. The issue is one purpose. How do you teach the path of purpose to your children? I may not have devoted myself to my children, but my heart is not like that. My heart is not like that. When God sees that, as long as it does not go against that principle, even if it does not go well, the descendants of that family will naturally be protected by God. Isn’t that right? Do you understand what I mean?

Do not say that you could not become a loving parent. If that parent has become a loyal subject, do not say that. Why? If the children of a loyal subject grow up without receiving their parents' love, then the king of that nation, the lord of that nation…
is a natural part of life. Do you understand? You may not receive the grace of your parents, but you can receive the grace of the nation. Which is a blessing? If a child can receive the protection of the nation, then it is a blessing for the parents to go for their child. This is how it is. This is the principle and the official path. It is the way of the will. Do you understand? "Yes." It is the center. Direction, do not lose your direction whether it is day or night.

That is why the teacher has not prayed even once for my sons and daughters until now. If I were to pray like that, I would pray for the world. If the will of the world is fulfilled, then even though I have not prayed for my sons and daughters, as I mentioned earlier, they can participate in the victory first. Do you understand this? That is why God has not cared for His close sons and daughters until now. He has sacrificed them. However, on the day of God's glory, they can automatically participate. This is salvation.

Therefore, you must align everything, including blinking and breathing, with the direction of the center. Even after walking or running all day long, when you finally get to rest, you should think, "What have I done?" and keep your eyes open to think about the way of the will, the will. You should reflect on it. Even if you are resting, if you can look at the scenery, your heart will be at ease. If not, you must shed tears and repent. The teacher is living this kind of life.

That is why you must always focus all your nerves on aligning with the center and direction. Knowing that it is a dangerous reality where you could derail at any moment, I hope you can become those who can adjust your lives for the sake of the will.

8) The Providential Present Moment
After the teacher returned to the country, please raise your hands if you are seeing someone for the first time. Many people used to come in the past. Put your hands down. Please raise your hands if you are from blessed families. Blessed families... Put your hands down.

The title may be a bit difficult, but it is called ‘The Providential Present Moment’... Providence refers to God's salvation providence up to now. It refers to the path of God's will to save humanity. In light of that path, it means the present moment, that is, this time. Providential present moment!

God's Providence to Establish Humanity
It is often said in the world that no matter how much of a hero one may be, if the time does not come, one cannot fulfill the will. We often hear that when a talented person appears on a prepared foundation, that person and the time combine to create a new history. We know this well through history. Therefore, the issue of time is always a problem.

In the morning, we wake up, eat breakfast, and start working. Then, when lunchtime comes, we must eat lunch. After lunch, we start the afternoon work. Again, when evening comes, we eat dinner and welcome the night. In this way, we live our lives facing new changing environments centered around some regular time.

Looking at ourselves, we have a boyhood, a youth, and after youth comes adulthood, and after adulthood comes old age. Through this process, one completes a life. That life is never constant. Whether in boyhood, youth, adulthood, or old age, if one mismanages the time, it can lead to the regret of wishing one had never been born.

However, if one lives meaningfully by managing the time well in boyhood, youth, adulthood, or old age, that person's life can remain as the most precious life. Therefore, if one mismanages the time, the motivation for failure begins there, and if one manages the time well, it becomes the starting point for success, which we can clearly understand from our daily lives.

Then, what kind of being is God? Of course, He is the Absolute Being. Everything He has planned has been fulfilled, and everything must be fulfilled, and He is the one who fulfills it. Therefore, if God were to carry out this providence alone, there would be no problem. Because He is the Absolute Being, once He starts, there is nothing that cannot be done. Everything that starts ends in success. In other words, if God were to carry out the providence alone, there would be no problem, but we know that providence cannot be fulfilled by God alone.

Why is that? To save fallen humanity, humans must indemnify their own sins because they have committed them. Isn’t it the same in the world? If a child commits a crime, the parents cannot serve the sentence in place of the child. Parents cannot indemnify the sins. The one who committed the sin must pay the price for it. We know this well when we look at the affairs of this world. Similarly, because humans have fallen, God cannot lead the fallen humanity to salvation. Even in carrying out the providential will, God must place humans in front and allow them to cooperate with the will of providence.

God has always worked through humans as representatives of the external aspect while being present in the internal aspect. In establishing people to work, it is not done blindly but is always done under a certain plan, preparing a time and finding suitable people to fulfill it. 

For example, after the fall of Adam, God prepared for 1600 years to establish Noah. Although God worked for 1600 years, to determine whether the fruits of that labor would be fulfilled, one person had to be established. Therefore, God had to establish one person, Noah. However, even though God had worked throughout that entire period, it would have been nice if Noah could inherit the glory of that effort, but even after choosing Noah, God did not allow him to live a glorious life. We know that God pushed Noah into an incomprehensible position. He commanded him to build an ark on the top of Mount Ararat. Normally, one would build a boat by the riverside or the seaside, but instead, God commanded him to build it on a mountain top, which is something that ordinary people would find unbelievable.

Moreover, even Noah, who had to bear a global responsibility, was placed in a position where he could only doubt it. However, we know that Noah believed the unbelievable command and devoted all his loyalty to building the ark for 120 years, overcoming difficult circumstances. We must understand that there was never a joyful time for Noah during that period. While building the ark was indeed precious, we must also recognize that Noah's mental attitude during the daily life of building the ark was even more critical.

Let’s imagine that there is such a grandfather in Korea, where thirty million people live. It doesn’t matter if he is in Chungcheong Province or Gangwon Province; anywhere is fine. If someone says, "There is a man building a boat on the top of a mountain," would you believe that? You would say, "That crazy guy! Don’t even talk about it." You would think, "Where could such a person be?" and treat anyone who says that as a madman. If you treat the person who says it as a madman, then the person actually doing it would be treated even more as a madman. Anyone who sees that normally would think that person is insane.

Heaven prepared a long time of 1600 years to provide such a moment. God, who must establish one person and command him to do that work, has reasons that prevent Him from giving normal commands. 

Now, why must it be this way? If it were just God and humans, the problem would be simple. God desires to fulfill the providential will by establishing people, so He must want people to fulfill the will above all else. However, why can’t He place them in such positions? If He is omniscient and omnipotent, why can’t He do that? When we look at this issue, it is not that simple.

If the true God says, "I will do this," then it must be done. Such a God did not create humans to fall. He created them so that they would not fall. Because humans have fallen, what God said He would do could not be done. Who is to blame for this inability? It is not God but humans. What about humans prevented it? It was disbelief that prevented it. Because they could not believe, they could not achieve it.

What they believed was something that could be believed from a normal position. Adam and Eve should have believed what they could naturally believe, but they could not. In other words, they could not believe what they should have believed from a normal position. Therefore, to restore this, they must believe from a position where it is not normal. They sinned from a normal position, but to indemnify that sin, they must indemnify it from an abnormal position. Isn’t that right?

If you commit a crime, you must serve a sentence of five years or ten years in prison. Serving a sentence is not normal; it is abnormal. In prison, the system does not allow freedom, and one must look at their own position and endure until the term is over to be liberated.

In this light, when God presented such a command to Noah, it was not because He hated Noah but to correct the fundamental principle that had gone awry due to the fall. We must understand how miserable God's heart was that He could not help but give such a command. We must realize how miserable God's internal heart was that did not want to do this but had no choice.

Noah's Courage and Patience
Noah must have faced many circumstances when he was lonely, when he was in difficulty, when he was sad, and when he was extremely isolated. What do you think he thought during those times? There must have been many moments when he felt like quitting that work. However, if he had not had a foundation of internal victory to overcome those moments, Noah would have flowed into history as a failed figure.

However, every time difficulties confronted Noah, he renewed his determination and resolution internally. What was that? "God is undoubtedly a being of certainty. The fact that He commanded me and placed me in this position is not to bring me down but to fulfill a deep purpose that the people of the world cannot achieve through me." Because he had this internal resolution and heart stronger than anyone else, we must understand that he continued to fulfill the mission of a pioneer day by day, even in the face of difficulties.

After about ten years, the people who opposed him probably stopped paying attention to Noah. After about twenty years, they might not have even looked at him. So what was the biggest problem? While the opposition from the townspeople might not have been a problem, the biggest issue was within his own family. If he had a mother, a wife, or children, then his family would be the problem. If Noah had a mother, would she have praised him? She would have opposed him. What about Noah's wife? She would have opposed him as well. What about his sons and daughters? They would have opposed him too. They would surely have said, "Our father has gone mad."

If Noah had been affected by such opposition from his family, God's will would have been frustrated there. Even if his beloved wife opposed him, he needed the conviction to overcome this and push forward.
If Noah had not been able to endure, he would not have overcome that environment. Even if his beloved sons and daughters opposed him, if he did not have the confidence to overcome this and did not have a self-awareness, he would have been broken in that environment.

Now, if his wife had started to oppose him and not listen, would Noah have been properly clothed? Would he have been properly fed? Think about it. If Grandpa Noah slept in the lower room, his wife would want to sleep in the upper room, and there would have been constant conflicts.

However, after a year, two years, three years in such an environment, when they realized that opposing him would not lead to any result, they would stop opposing him. They oppose when there is a possibility of breaking him, but when there is no possibility at all, even the wife and children do not oppose. We can glimpse here that God's will and hope remain only after passing through a phase where there is no longer any opposition.

The people in the neighborhood would have opposed him and then all become exhausted and fallen away, and his own sons and daughters would have opposed him and then become exhausted and fallen away, and even his wife would have opposed him and then become exhausted and fallen away. So, if there were still someone who could oppose him, who would that person be? The people close to him would have all become exhausted and fallen away. If there were still someone who could oppose him, it would be the country. They might say, "You, this old man, the actions you are taking are actions that will ruin our people and nation." If there was a king at that time, he would have opposed him with royal authority. Wouldn't that be the case? If that were so, what should Grandpa Noah have done? At that time, it was not a matter of a difficult environment, but rather a determination to overcome it, even if it meant risking his life.

Satan knew well that God was establishing Grandpa Noah for a great providence. Satan knew that the day Noah would win according to God's will would be the day the world of Satan would collapse. So, Satan devised various schemes, saying, "God, this Grandpa Noah has not heard the opposition from the villagers. He has not heard the opposition from his own sons and daughters. He has not heard the opposition from his beloved wife. However, if the king of the nation wields power and threatens to cut off his head, he will surely abandon God's will and flee." This is how Satan would slander.

So why is that? Grandpa Noah's intention was not just to save one family. Of course, he needed to save his family, but it was also to save the nation and to take away the entire world of Satan to establish the heavenly world. Therefore, Satan could attack Grandpa Noah with such a significant condition.

What would Grandpa Noah have thought? Have you ever thought about that? "Grandpa Noah has worked hard for 120 years building the ark, and now the day of the launch is just around the corner. It is the day when the 120-year period is complete." What would have happened the day before that, when the country was mobilized to cut off Noah's head? If it were time for judgment, rather than the flood judgment, how would he have reacted? If Noah were an ordinary person, he might have thought, "God is indifferent..."

After suffering for 120 years, now with nothing left but his old body, and thinking that God, who had never shown him compassion, would finally show compassion and that he could wait with hope for the launch, but then a wicked king threatens to cut off his head, how would Grandpa Noah have felt? That would be astonishing, wouldn't it?

If Satan knew that it would be a big problem if Noah won, he would have tried to strangle Noah. Responding to Satan's slander, God might have said, "Go ahead and do as you wish." Then Satan would have used the wicked king under his command to say, "What you are doing is ruining the nation, and everything you have done cannot be forgiven by this nation and people." When they tried to cut off Noah's head, what would Grandpa Noah have had to do? Should he retreat or push forward? Answer me. "He must go forward." Yes, he must go forward, but is that an easy thing?

Some people in the Unification Church say, "I have believed for 10 years." Others say, "I have believed for 20 years." Those who have believed for 20 years think they no longer need to evangelize. They plan to say, "I have done enough evangelizing, so I should take a break." When God gives another command, if they respond with, "That command is just whatever," what happens? Can such a person stand as a qualified person to face God's will? That is the issue. Even if only one day remains, you must understand that until the moment of completion, all problems remain unresolved. Grandpa Noah must have started his work with the determination, "Even if I do not succeed and die, I will die cleanly." He might have thought, "Even if I die, if I cannot finish it alone, God will mobilize ten or a hundred people to finish it." If Noah had that thought, he would have been excited. He might have thought, "I hope I die quickly while building this ark." When there is no possibility of completing it alone after 120 years, he would have worked hard, aiming for the time of death, thinking that if he died in the middle of it, comrades who could help complete it would emerge quickly.

If Noah had the heart of believing in the absolute God, he would have thought that dying was not the end but rather a new beginning. He might have thought, "Isn't this place of death simpler and happier than going through a long path of suffering?"

With such thoughts, if he had finished building the ark and was told to die just two days before the launch, it would be a position where one could think that God is indifferent. If he had been told to die ten or twenty years after starting to build the ark, it might have been different, but now, just two days before completion, most people would complain and resent. Don't you think so? Deep down, they might think that even if the world perishes, they would survive, but when faced with death, would they not complain? What would you do? Honestly, answer! "I would complain." Yes, they would complain. When they complain and oppose, what happens to the will and everything else? It becomes zero. It definitely becomes zero. Then, they might think, "It would have been better not to have done it at all; what is this?" Such a situation could arise.

The Greatness of Abraham

Now, let's stop talking about Grandpa Noah and move on to Abraham. Abraham is also a grandfather. In the past, it was all the age of grandfathers. Nowadays, in the Unification Church era, it is not the age of grandfathers; what age do we call it? "The age of youth." The age of youth, so grandfathers should not feel disappointed. When the youth fight and win, they bring the prize to the grandfathers. That is how it should be. Do not feel disappointed.

Grandpa Abraham was living well in his hometown of Ur of the Chaldeans when God called him out and led him around as a foreigner, asking him to offer sacrifices. Did Abraham say, "God! I have prepared the altar for the sacrifice; will you accept it or not?" He did not even pray. He did not ask for it, but God came and said, "You have worked hard, so I will bless you. Your descendants will be more prosperous than the stars in the sky and the sand on the ground, so offer the three generations of sacrifices." That is why he offered sacrifices.

When he was about to offer sacrifices and was splitting the offerings, would it have been a big deal if he had not split a small dove? Isn't that right? Is there a place to put a knife to split that little dove? If he had not split it, it would have been fine. Was he that upset? The God who promised to bless him would not have said, "Your descendants will serve as slaves for 400 years!" if he had not split the dove. Would he have recognized that God was God? He might have thought, "This is not Satan!"

However, what was the greatness of Grandpa Abraham? He feared that more than anything else. When God would impose such a punishment, he considered it more serious than his own death. That is why Grandpa Abraham is great.

Even after making such a mistake and being in a place of great shock, he had the heart to serve God. So when he received the command to sacrifice his son, he resolved to act immediately if he could resolve the shock of having to sacrifice his son. We must understand how carefully he considered the words that God commanded him. That is why he was able to offer his son, who was obtained miraculously as a blessing at the age of 100. How could he believe that after receiving a son, he would have to sacrifice him again? It is all contradictory. It is absolutely not something that can be done with human reasoning.

Even the father of the fallen world would not do such a thing if he blessed someone, let alone God. There is a twist here that we humans do not understand. Generally, humans cannot love beyond themselves. They cannot think beyond themselves. No matter whom they love, they do not want to love without including themselves. They try to love while adding themselves. Humans do not want to move anything by denying themselves. Nevertheless, Abraham chose the path of love from a position of self-denial. What love did he seek by denying himself? He sought God's love. He denied himself, denied his clan, and denied his relatives. What family and what clan did he seek? He sought a family that could please God and a clan that could please God, even if the world opposed him. We must understand that Abraham was the representative who envisioned that.

Even if it meant sacrificing his own child, he deeply wished for a clan and a nation that could please God. Because that desire was greater than any difficult circumstance… Abraham was able to break through the many hardships of a nomadic life. Because that desire was great, and because his heart of love was always strong, and because he was firmly determined to live for that, he was able to set aside all difficult circumstances and follow only the path that God directed. Not only that, but later he even found himself in a position where he lost his wife in Egypt.

Now, at that time, how much would Abraham have resented God? He was taken from his home, and then he lost his wife to Pharaoh; everything had gone wrong. However, Abraham did not resent Pharaoh for taking Sarah. He thought, "Heaven! What will happen next? Surely you love me, and you would not set me up for such a thing to make me suffer." 

If Abraham had complained after losing Sarah, saying, "God is indifferent; you told me to leave my house and made me live as a wanderer for decades, and now I have lost my wife and am completely cornered in a foreign land. Resentful God!" and had slandered God, what would have happened? "Love, will, I do not know anything. Whether God exists or not, I do not know. This is becoming more and more overwhelming." If he had slandered like that, what would have happened? There would have been no conditions to believe.

However, what was admirable about Abraham was that he believed unconditionally. If he had lost his wife and prayed in a complaining manner, "God, please find my wife," what would have happened to Sarah? Would God have found her? Surely Satan would have tightened his grip on Sarah. However, the reason God was able to take Sarah away from Pharaoh's arms was that God was moved, and even Satan, who was slandering, was moved. Only when God could bless in a position where Satan's glaring scrutiny was rendered powerless could it become a blessing of pride and not a blessing of slander. You must understand that God wanted to deal with Abraham in such a position.

Abraham was not in a position of opposition but rather said, "When you lead my family out for your will, I have already resolved to sacrifice everything, including my life. I am grateful just to have lived until now. I have only the heart to serve you, so if you have a purpose you want to achieve, please handle it as you wish. Please do according to your profound will." Abraham believed that if he could fulfill the heavenly will by sacrificing Sarah, there would be no greater blessing. If he had prayed from a position of opposition, it would have been impossible. Sarah would surely have become a concubine in Pharaoh's palace.

The attitude of Abraham himself, who was the subject, toward God's will, and his attitude of handling difficult circumstances at that time, was the attitude that the enemy could not establish conditions for slander. God, who knows human circumstances well but commands with a heart full of tears, wanted to embrace him even more intensely in difficult situations, and this stimulated the heart of God to give everything. From there, through Abraham, who became a descendant of disbelief, a new heart of righteousness and compassion could arise, and thus the work of heaven could remain on earth.

You must understand this. If that is not present, it is just as it is. There is nothing different from the world of Satan. You must recognize the greatness of Abraham. Because Abraham, whom God led out, had such a great heart and overcame all periods of trial, he became Abraham, who was worthy of receiving even greater blessings. If we were to talk about this, there would be no end.

Moses, who Respected the Chosen People More Than Anyone Else

Now, let’s look at Moses. Moses, who enjoyed the luxurious glory of a prince in Pharaoh's palace, could have thought that the suffering of the Israelites was none of his business. If the Israelites fought among themselves, he could have ignored it, and that would have been the end of it. However, Moses respected and revered the chosen people of heaven more than any nation or people. That is where the value lies.

In other words, Moses valued the chosen people established by heaven more than any sovereign nation's prince or the entire sovereign nation. You must understand that this is the motivation for why heaven viewed Moses as great.

Moses did not see the miserable individual of Israel, who was being whipped by the Egyptians and was under the command of the Egyptian people, as just an individual. "On my path, the kingdom of God will eventually sprout. When that individual stands in a position of injustice, I must not be a bystander."
Yes. "Heaven will surely be with those who advocate for and support them. If you are willing to risk your life for them, heaven will surely be with you." This is the belief that Moses had when he took responsibility and stepped forward. It started from such motivation. Therefore, he became one who sided with Israel and killed an Egyptian. He did not kill the Egyptian out of his own emotions, but to elevate God's will, hoping for a smooth path for God in the future, wishing for a foundation of victory for heaven, and desiring that heaven could rule even Egypt with a victorious sovereignty, acting with the heart of wanting to be a loyal subject and patriot of that country. That is why Moses is not bound by the law. He does not receive accusations from Satan. Although the land is the world of Satan, the enemy of Israel, and the territory governed by that nation, a person who acts with a heart of loyalty to heaven, striving solely to establish heaven and fighting with the determination to risk his life for the sovereignty of that nation cannot be anything but a patriot. 

If there is a path of hardship in fighting from such a position, it is the path of a patriot's hardship. If there is a nation and its sovereignty, it must be defended and protected. Such responsibility lies with heaven, and that is only natural. Even if Moses could not think that deeply, heaven, looking at Moses's loyalty, integrity, and steadfastness, recognized that his actions stemmed from a love for the Israelite people and a patriotism that envisioned a blessed future nation, and could not help but sympathize with him. That is why, even during the 40 years Moses lived alone as a shepherd in the Midian wilderness, God always protected him.

Moses, who had the source and motivation to receive heaven's sympathy at the right time, never forgot that he killed the Egyptian even during his 40 years in the Midian wilderness. "Because I killed the Egyptian, I am living a miserable life in the wilderness, but that is because I love my country. Even if my life ends, I cannot forget my love for my country." This was undoubtedly Moses's traditional thought. His daily life would have been impoverished, and the environment he faced would have been dangerous and restrictive. The more he was cornered by such an environment, the more he must have recalled the past. To become one with the miserable Israelite people, he must have made a resolution that said, "Even if I am driven out from here, even if I give up everything, I cannot abandon my love for my country." After making such a resolution, he must have carried out such actions. It was all for heaven and for the Israelite people, which is why God could not abandon that patriot who loved Israel.

Therefore, the more Moses faced bitter circumstances during his 40 years in the wilderness, the more loneliness filled his life, and the more tears came from his environment. The harsher and more difficult that environment became, the more the heart of heaven's sympathy grew stronger behind it, and we must recognize that there was an inner connection. Moses, even when lying alone at night, could not forget his heart for the nation of Israel. In the midst of his weary daily life, he did not blame anyone but held a heart that blamed Egypt. He did not perceive all the stimuli that came to him as personal suffering but lived with a heart that hated the sovereign of evil that drove humanity into hardship. Because of this, even after 40 years, God raised Moses again. In searching for someone who could save Israel, there was no one with a belief greater than Moses or someone who cared for the nation and sovereignty of Israel more than he did. Thus, even though he lived a humble life as a shepherd, God could not help but awaken Moses and set him as the one responsible for saving Israel.

So, what kind of life was Moses's 40 years as a shepherd? It was a preparatory life to lead the chosen people of Israel, a period of training and trial to cultivate the strength to overcome the suffering path that lay ahead. That is why you must understand that God sent Moses again before the Israelite people. 

Then, what allowed Moses to continue the connection of God's blessings from his lonely position? It was because he loved the hopeful nation of Israel and made the protection of the hopeful Israelite people the object of his pursuit beyond his living environment, that he could smoothly endure the difficult 40 years in the Midian wilderness. If he had thought even a little about his past, he would have dreamed of the luxurious life in the palace and longed for that environment. The greater the difference compared to his current situation, the more sorrowful he would have become. However, because Moses stood in a position where he did not even think of such things, a connection was woven that could call him back to the position of the master of the Israelite people from a place of abandonment.

Outwardly, Moses appeared to have completely lost his timing. He lost his timing in the palace and lived alone for 40 years in the Midian wilderness without being able to find the right time before heaven. However, Moses had the hope of waiting for the day promised by heaven, a heart to save the Israelite people, and a steadfastness to overcome the lost time and environment. Because of this, he was able to bind Israel again and save the nation of Israel.

In doing this, how close must his inner feelings have been to God! There were countless emotional connections behind it that made it impossible for God not to sympathize with him. A person standing in such a position must inevitably be given a time that represents heaven, and it is heaven's will that this must happen.

Our historical ancestors have inherited the meaning of historical connections like this. When viewed this way, the representative of our ancestors who inherited such a foundation of blessings in the providential historical era did not have a smooth path. Since the day we believed in the Unification Church, it is not that we simply welcomed the time of blessings with the resolution of "Now that I know this path, I will surely go." You must understand that to welcome the time of blessings, one must go through many paths of suffering. Historical ancestors also presented all conditions for indemnity and, after surpassing all conditions of Satan's accusations, only those with loyalty who overcame without being caught in accusations could welcome the time of blessings. You must understand that.

Look at someone like John the Baptist. John the Baptist was born amidst the commotion of towns and villages. The townspeople's interest was focused on the question, "What will this child become when he grows up?" Moreover, being born into the family of the high priest Zechariah, how well he must have grown! How much love must he have received from his mother and father? Yet, John the Baptist left home. He went to the wilderness and lived for 30 years eating locusts and wild honey.

Today, young men and women of the Unification Church may hear the townspeople say, "That guy said he was going to college, but look at him now!" or "That so-and-so's daughter was said to be talented, but look at her now! She has turned out like this! It's because her parents are like that; the offspring follows the lineage..." There may be people who hear all kinds of criticisms. "That guy will just end up like that! What can you do? It's been 10 years since he joined the Unification Church, and look at him now; his face is gaunt, and his eyes are bulging..." This is indeed a pitiful sight.

Yet, if you look closely, his eyes are still alive. That is what matters. If even those eyes were to become dull, and he lost all vitality, that would not be acceptable. Now, when you think about it, how much suffering have you endured since joining the Unification Church? Think about it. Those who have been in the Unification Church for over 10 years, raise your hands! There aren’t many. Oh, if you raised your hands, why are you doing it like that? What is this? Can you see me? Raise your hands clearly! Put them down. It’s not many at all. Not even a fifth of you.

Now, among those who have been here for over 10 years, there will be some who say, "I have suffered since joining the Unification Church..." Then, consider how much suffering you have really endured. Compared to the patriots who traversed Manchuria or the Siberian plains during the colonial era, this is nothing. Did you have guns and swords following you? Did you ever experience the situation where you would die if you were caught? What you have done is merely a game of saying, "If I don’t like it, I won’t do it; if I like it, I will." This is the so-called Unification Church crowd. Those who say, "If I don’t like it, I won’t do it; if I like it, I will," cannot absolutely fulfill their purpose. It is destined to fail.

Now! If Grandpa Noah were like you, would he have gone out for 20 years? Forget 20 years, would he have gone out for even 3 years? He would not have. But did Grandpa Noah go out knowing the principles of the Unification Church, saying, "This is how it should be done, and this is how it should not be done"? No, Grandpa Noah was not that meticulous. One day, God appeared to him in a dream and said, "Noah, in 120 years, I will make you the master and judge all the people of the world, so build an ark." From that day on, he worked on the ark every day for 120 years. He was not told, "After one year, there will be 119 years left." After 10 years, he was not told, "There are 110 years left, so come on!" If he had been told that, it would have been a big problem.

Why? If God is absolute, then you must believe absolutely. If you go every day and say, "Hey! You did that yesterday, but you shouldn’t do it like that today," is that a position of absolute belief? No, it is a position of not believing absolutely. Therefore, for God to be the subject who can be believed absolutely and for the counterpart to believe absolutely before that subject, He must give a command just once, and that must be absolute. If that is the case, would God come to encourage Noah every day for 120 years? No, that would not happen. Yet, because Noah believed absolutely for 120 years, he is considered great.

Today, you in the Unification Church have a teacher who speaks about the providential historical moment and various matters, but did people back then know such things? They did not. When you look at this, you must recognize that there is an immeasurable difference between your current situation and the foundation that our ancestors have expanded upon throughout historical eras.

The Life of John the Baptist
I have taught you the principles too meticulously. Because I told you to use all your fingers and toes at once, they are all becoming numb, and you can only use one at a time. Do you understand what I mean?

In a hurry, I taught you everything from world restoration to the restoration of the cosmos at once, but many have become numb and unable to use everything because they were told to do it all at once without rest. Do you understand what I mean? If I had taught you little by little, giving you just a bit of the fall theory first, and then a little more as you were dying, and then just a bit for your eyes, and then a bit for your nose, and then a bit for your head, teaching you gradually, you would not have become exhausted. But because I told you to swallow it all at once, you have become sick and have experienced all sorts of troubles. Many have become ill because they could not digest what was good medicine that was wrapped up. However, those who can digest it will be able to walk the right path.

Now, when you compare yourselves in the Unification Church with Noah, Abraham, or John the Baptist from the past, who is more blessed? Who is more blessed? You in the Unification Church are the blessed ones. The time of blessings has indeed come. Look! The precious John the Baptist ate locusts and wild honey every day. But did locusts just come flying into his mouth while he sat still? (Laughter) So he had to run around in the fields to catch them. Think about it. Does that seem impressive? When his parents and relatives saw him like that, would they have been astonished or not? Think about it. How astonishing it must have been. How much did he have to wander around the rocks to get wild honey? It sounds impressive, but when you look at the reality, it seems like he was a madman.

If you go to Israel, you will see that there are not many wild honey and locusts. It is half a desert area. It is a desert area. Nowadays, there is probably not even a blade of grass; everything is dried up. This begins to dry up from May, passing through September, October, November, December, January, February, March, April. When we went recently, it was just starting to dry up. It is an astonishing place.

Now, would the parents' hearts have been pleased when they saw such a sight? That kid, "I thought he would become a dragon, but he turned out to be a pupa." There is a saying, right? A pupa? (Laughter) I thought he would become a dragon, but he turned out to be a pupa. Not a pupa that would become a butterfly, but a pupa that could not even become a butterfly. How astonishing that must have been!

Also, from John the Baptist's perspective, he must have thought, "When will this end? Today is just like tomorrow..." When he thought about it, it must have felt endless. This is not like an appendicitis surgery where you have to resolve it within 24 hours. There is no such refreshing restoration history where you can just cut it open quickly. It is just tedious, dragging on. But you must not die either.

John the Baptist himself must have been astonished. He was wandering around the wilderness with a bundle, waiting for the Messiah to come, not knowing when He would arrive. He had no idea that his cousin, Jesus, whom he had never even dreamed of, would suddenly appear. The Holy Spirit descended upon his cousin like a dove, revealing that Jesus was the Messiah. Knowing the history of his cousin well, he must have been astonished that the one born as an illegitimate child, the son of an insignificant family in his town, was the Messiah. 

There is a reason why the astonishing content is astonishing. (Laughter) Those who have tasted the astonishing flavor know it well. Extremes connect. You have tasted the bitter.
Did you see it? It's bitter. A while ago, Mr. Lee brought me some gall and I thought, "How bitter can it be?" So I took a tiny bit and put it in my mouth. As a man, I couldn't spit it out after putting it in, so I had no choice but to swallow it. After that, I was nearly in tears from how bitter it was. (Laughter) Then you will understand. After feeling such bitterness, I rinsed my mouth with water, opened the door, let in the cold wind, and took a breath of fresh air, and this time, mysteriously, I tasted sweetness. It's strange, isn't it? Ah! That's why this becomes medicine... I thought. If it were just bitter, people would reject it and not cling to it, but because there is some factor that allows it to stick, because there is something that can be absorbed, I believe it becomes medicine.

That's why extremes? "Connect." They connect. If you enter a place of ruin? It's one of two things: either you will not perish, or you will prosper. That's why I think God calculated well. If there is a way for a fallen group to enter a place of ruin and possibly prosper, would He not put them there? There is a chance of luck. Even if everything perishes, if you can be in a position where you will not perish, a way to prosper opens up. God has been carrying out the restoration history under such a resolve.

If I keep talking like this, there will be no end, so let's return to the topic of the Unification Church.

Historically, all our ancestors lived such lives. John the Baptist testified to the Messiah, but where did he do it? He did it by the Jordan River. When someone was sick and near death, the song that Christians sang was, "We will meet beyond the Jordan River, a few days later, a few days later, we will meet beyond the Jordan River." (Laughter) Just how exciting and wonderful is the Jordan River that they say, "Let's meet beyond the Jordan River"? There are meadows and flower fields, and the Jordan River is so clear that all the birds passing by would want to come and bathe in it. That's what people think, right? "Yes." It is absolutely the opposite. When I looked into it, I thought, "Ah! This is why it's called the Jordan River!" (Laughter) I thought of it more as a noisy river. It's astonishing. The muddy water flows out from the long stretches of the desert, through the sands of the desert, and it has become what it is.

When I first went to the Jordan River, I was so happy that I thought I would wash my face in that river, but I couldn't wash at all. It's astonishing. I thought the Jordan River was very large, but how big is it? It seemed just right for big kids to swim across. Now! In the Bible, it says that the Holy Spirit descended like a dove and said, "This is my beloved Son." That's why the Jordan River looks so wonderful...

Also, in the desert area, do you think Jesus appeared dressed like a prince in fine clothes? Think about it. Jesus surely lived poorly as Joseph's son, so his situation must have been quite miserable. (Laughter) That younger brother, the guy you see, must have had a miserable situation. He must have gone out to the wilderness to pray, and things must have happened that made him look miserable.

In such a situation, when he saw someone walking hesitantly to be baptized, what do you think John the Baptist felt? John the Baptist knew well about Jesus' history. He knew that Jesus was an illegitimate child, not Joseph's son. He must have thought, "Why is that illegitimate child showing up to make me feel uncomfortable!" But God taught him, so he had no choice but to baptize him, yet afterward, he must have been astonished. Just think about it.

For John the Baptist, it was something he could not even imagine. He could never have dreamed that he would have to welcome Jesus, who grew up in such an environment, as the Messiah. This is not just a small deviation in imagination. So, do you think his eyes opened wide? They must have opened wide before he even realized it. Would he have felt good or bad? He must have felt bad.

Since there was a command from God, he couldn't refuse, so after baptizing him, it became a mystery. That's why later, when he was imprisoned, he sent two disciples to Jesus to ask, "Should we wait for another, or are you the one who is to come?" This shows that John the Baptist never thought it would turn out this way.

When I think that what I prepared for 30 years was just to baptize Jesus, John the Baptist must have been astonished. He must have thought that our family was completely ruined. You must understand that history has developed and connected through such stories. Do you understand? "Yes."

When looking at God's will, has there ever been a historical precedent where the will was fulfilled in a place that seemed likely? "No." You must understand that there has never been a history where the will was fulfilled in a place that seemed likely or could have been likely. Everything is negative, everything is miserable, everything is misunderstood, everything seems to be unreal, and from such places, history has been connected. So, is it likely to succeed every time, or likely to fail? "Likely to fail." 

That's why it is likely to fail every time. You must understand this.

The Path Christians Must Take

The people of South Korea must move toward the North, yet they have failed to do so, so we must become a group that moves inwardly toward that direction. We must not engage in the foolishness of relocating our wives, husbands, and children but must establish a path of obedience in the face of this historical demand, becoming the sons and daughters of heaven who set a new historical tradition that will remain forever in the construction of heaven.  
On this day, may you be with all gathered here this evening, and having made new resolutions and pledges, even if we return to our original places, we must not rest. Just as heaven does not rest in its work while Satan also does not cease its opposition, we too must not rest but dedicate ourselves 24 hours a day to fulfill the mission of the new era that connects the nation and the world. Father, we earnestly ask you to push us forward, even if it means using a whip.  
We are those who have sworn to be offered as a sacrifice on the day of victory that heaven can rejoice in, so we earnestly request that you fulfill your will as you have permitted.  
As we give thanks for today's gathering, we hope that the blessings you grant in the future will be with us. We offer all these words in the name of True Parents. Amen.  
**Selected Words of Reverend Sun Myung Moon, Volume 57**
